href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8A%E8%90%AC%C2%B7%E5%85%8B%E9%9B%B7%E6%B4%9B%E5%A4%AB" title="伊万·克雷洛夫">伊万·克雷洛夫</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%89%E5%B8%83%E7%BD%97%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%AF%94%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF" title="安布罗斯·比尔斯">安布罗斯·比尔斯</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.88.B2.E5.8A.87.E8.A9.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="戏剧诗">戏剧诗</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="编辑章节：戏剧诗">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Verse drama and dramatic verse" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="诗歌戏剧与戏剧诗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A9%A9%E6%AD%8C%E6%88%B2%E5%8A%87%E8%88%87%E6%88%B2%E5%8A%87%E8%A9%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="诗歌戏剧与戏剧诗（页面不存在）">诗歌戏剧与戏剧诗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Verse_drama_and_dramatic_verse" title="en:Verse drama and dramatic verse"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Verse drama and dramatic verse</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%85%8A%E6%88%8F%E5%89%A7" title="古希腊戏剧">古希腊戏剧</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Indian classical drama" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="印度传统戏剧"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%B0%E5%BA%A6%E5%82%B3%E7%B5%B1%E6%88%B2%E5%8A%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="印度传统戏剧（页面不存在）">印度传统戏剧</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indian_classical_drama" title="en:Indian classical drama"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Indian classical drama</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%8F%E6%9B%B2" title="戏曲">戏曲</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%BD%E5%89%A7" title="能剧">能剧</a></div>
<p>戏剧诗是由供演员念读或唱出的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9F%BB%E6%96%87" title="韵文">韵文</a>写成的<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%B2%E5%8A%87" title="戏剧">戏剧</a>。在不同的文化中，戏剧诗会以不同的形式与形态出现。在诗歌中的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%85%8A%E6%82%B2%E5%89%A7" title="古希腊悲剧">古希腊悲剧</a>可追溯至公元前六世纪，而此或对印度传统戏剧的发展带来影响<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50">[48]</a></sup>，正如印度戏剧辗转对中国的<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%8A%E6%96%87" title="变文">变文</a>诗歌戏剧（现今<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%8F%E6%9B%B2" title="戏曲">戏曲</a>的前身）之发展带来影响。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51">[49]</a></sup><a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%9C%E4%BA%9A" title="东亚">东亚地区</a>的诗歌戏剧亦包括日本的<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%BD%E5%89%A7" title="能剧">能剧</a>。在<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%A2%E6%96%AF%E6%96%87%E5%AD%A6" title="波斯文学">波斯文学</a>中，戏剧诗的例子包括<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E6%89%8E%E7%B1%B3" title="尼扎米">尼扎米</a>的两套着名戏剧作品—《<a href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E6%8B%89%E5%92%8C%E7%8E%9B%E5%90%89%E5%8A%AA" title="莱拉和玛吉努">莱拉和玛吉努</a>》和《<a href="/wiki/%E9%9C%8D%E6%96%AF%E5%8B%9E%E5%92%8C%E5%B8%AD%E7%90%B3" title="霍斯劳和席琳">霍斯劳和席琳</a>》、<a href="/wiki/%E8%8F%B2%E7%88%BE%E5%A4%9A%E8%A5%BF" title="菲尔多西">菲尔多西</a>的悲剧作品如《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sohrab" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="索赫拉布"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B4%A2%E8%B5%AB%E6%8B%89%E5%B8%83&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="索赫拉布（页面不存在）">罗斯塔姆和索赫拉布</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sohrab" title="en:Sohrab"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sohrab</span></a></span>）</span></span>》、<a href="/wiki/%E9%B2%81%E7%B1%B3" title="鲁米">鲁米</a>的《<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%9B%E6%96%AF%E7%BA%B3%E7%BB%B4" title="玛斯纳维">玛斯纳维</a>》、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fakhruddin As'ad Gurgani" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="法赫鲁丁·阿斯阿德·古尔加尼"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B3%95%E8%B5%AB%E9%AD%AF%E4%B8%81%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E6%96%AF%E9%98%BF%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E5%8F%A4%E7%88%BE%E5%8A%A0%E5%B0%BC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="法赫鲁丁·阿斯阿德·古尔加尼（页面不存在）">法赫鲁丁·阿斯阿德·古尔加尼</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fakhruddin_As%27ad_Gurgani" title="en:Fakhruddin As'ad Gurgani"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fakhruddin As'ad Gurgani</span></a></span>）</span></span>的悲剧作品《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Vis and Rāmin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="维斯和拉敏"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B6%AD%E6%96%AF%E5%92%8C%E6%8B%89%E6%95%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="维斯和拉敏（页面不存在）">维斯和拉敏</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vis_and_R%C4%81min" title="en:Vis and Rāmin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Vis and Rāmin</span></a></span>）</span></span>》，以及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Vahshi Bafqi" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="瓦希·巴夫奇"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%93%A6%E5%B8%8C%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E5%A4%AB%E5%A5%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="瓦希·巴夫奇（页面不存在）">瓦希·巴夫奇</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vahshi_Bafqi" title="en:Vahshi Bafqi"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Vahshi Bafqi</span></a></span>）</span></span>的作品《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Farhad" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="法哈德 (文学作品)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B3%95%E5%93%88%E5%BE%B7_(%E6%96%87%E5%AD%B8%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="法哈德 (文学作品)（页面不存在）">法哈德</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Farhad" title="en:Farhad"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Farhad</span></a></span>）</span></span>》。20世纪的美国诗人将戏剧诗复兴，当中包括<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E5%85%B9%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E5%BA%9E%E5%BE%B7" title="艾兹拉·庞德">艾兹拉·庞德</a>的《Sestina: Altaforte,》<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52">[50]</a></sup>和<a href="/wiki/T%C2%B7S%C2%B7%E8%89%BE%E7%95%A5%E7%89%B9" title="T·S·艾略特">T·S·艾略特</a>的《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="The Love Song of J. Alfred Prufrock" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="阿尔弗瑞德‧普鲁弗洛克的情歌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%BF%E7%88%BE%E5%BC%97%E7%91%9E%E5%BE%B7%E2%80%A7%E6%99%AE%E9%AD%AF%E5%BC%97%E6%B4%9B%E5%85%8B%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="阿尔弗瑞德‧普鲁弗洛克的情歌（页面不存在）">阿尔弗瑞德‧普鲁弗洛克的情歌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Love_Song_of_J._Alfred_Prufrock" title="en:The Love Song of J. Alfred Prufrock"><span dir="auto" lang="en">The Love Song of J. Alfred Prufrock</span></a></span>）</span></span>》。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[51]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54">[52]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.80.9D.E8.BE.A8.E8.A9.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="思辨诗">思辨诗</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="编辑章节：思辨诗">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Фантастическая поэзия" data-lang-code="ru" data-lang-name="俄语" data-orig-title="思辨诗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%9D%E8%BE%A8%E8%A9%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="思辨诗（页面不存在）">思辨诗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">俄语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A4%D0%B0%D0%BD%D1%82%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B8%D1%87%D0%B5%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B0%D1%8F_%D0%BF%D0%BE%D1%8D%D0%B7%D0%B8%D1%8F" title="ru:Фантастическая поэзия"><span dir="auto" lang="ru">Фантастическая поэзия</span></a></span>）</span></span></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Poe_1848.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="252" data-file-width="190" decoding="async" height="252" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/91/Edgar_Poe_1848.jpg" width="190"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Poe_1848.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E7%88%B1%E4%BC%A6%C2%B7%E5%9D%A1" title="爱伦·坡">爱伦·坡</a>有时会被视为「思辨诗之父」</div></div></div>
<p>思辨诗（又称「奇妙诗」，当中古怪诗或恐怖诗是其中一个主要子分类）是一种处理「超越现实」主题的诗歌体裁，而这些主题可以来自<a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%B9%BB%E5%B0%8F%E8%AF%B4" title="科幻小说">科幻小说</a>中的<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%96%E6%8E%A8" title="外推">外推</a>，又或<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Horror fiction" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="恐布小说"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%81%90%E4%BD%88%E5%B0%8F%E8%AA%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="恐布小说（页面不存在）">恐布小说</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horror_fiction" title="en:Horror fiction"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Horror fiction</span></a></span>）</span></span>中的怪异及可怕主题。这些诗作定期刊载于现代科幻小说作品及恐怖小说杂志中。有时候，<a href="/wiki/%E7%88%B1%E4%BC%A6%C2%B7%E5%9D%A1" title="爱伦·坡">爱伦·坡</a>会被视为「思辨诗之父」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[53]</a></sup>，皆因他在思辨诗体裁的贡献中，其中之一就是其在1848年的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9A%8F%E7%AC%94" title="随笔">随笔</a>（基于该作品的推测性质，他将之称作一则「<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%A3%E6%96%87%E8%A9%A9" title="散文诗">散文诗</a>」）《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Eureka: A Prose Poem" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尤里卡：散文诗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%A4%E9%87%8C%E5%8D%A1%EF%BC%9A%E6%95%A3%E6%96%87%E8%A9%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尤里卡：散文诗（页面不存在）">尤里卡：散文诗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eureka:_A_Prose_Poem" title="en:Eureka: A Prose Poem"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Eureka: A Prose Poem</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中，包含其对<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%87%E5%AE%99" title="宇宙">宇宙</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E7%88%86%E7%82%B8" title="大爆炸">大爆炸</a>起源之推测，而这推测比<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%94%E6%B2%BB%C2%B7%E5%8B%92%E6%A2%85%E7%89%B9" title="乔治·勒梅特">乔治·勒梅特</a>还要早四分之三个世纪。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[54]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[55]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.95.A3.E6.96.87.E8.A9.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="散文诗">散文诗</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="编辑章节：散文诗">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%A3%E6%96%87%E8%A9%A9" title="散文诗">散文诗</a></div>
<p>散文诗是一种结合散文与诗歌元素的混合体裁，或可能与<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%9E%8B%E5%B0%8F%E8%AF%B4" title="微型小说">微型小说</a>（又称「小小说」、「极短篇小说」）难以分辨。在现代读者角度而言，纵然部份早期散文例子或会解读成「诗歌」，「散文诗」的由来一般认为是始于19世纪的法国，而当时尝试过这类诗歌的诗人包括<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Aloysius Bertrand" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="阿洛伊修斯·贝尔特朗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%BF%E6%B4%9B%E4%BC%8A%E4%BF%AE%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E8%B2%9D%E7%88%BE%E7%89%B9%E6%9C%97&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="阿洛伊修斯·贝尔特朗（页面不存在）">阿洛伊修斯·贝尔特朗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aloysius_Bertrand" title="en:Aloysius Bertrand"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Aloysius Bertrand</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8F%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E6%B3%A2%E5%BE%B7%E8%8E%B1%E5%B0%94" title="夏尔·波德莱尔">夏尔·波德莱尔</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E8%92%82%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E5%85%B0%E6%B3%A2" title="阿蒂尔·兰波">阿蒂尔·兰波</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A6%AC%E6%8B%89%E7%BE%8E" title="马拉美">马拉美</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[56]</a></sup>尤自1980年代后期，散文诗逐渐受到读者欢迎，在《The Prose Poem: An International Journal》<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59">[57]</a></sup>、《Contemporary Haibun Online》<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[58]</a></sup>及《Haibun Today》<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[59]</a></sup>等全本式期刊中亦致力于该体裁及相关混合体。在20世纪，撰写散文诗的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Latin American poetry" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="拉丁美洲诗歌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%8B%89%E4%B8%81%E7%BE%8E%E6%B4%B2%E8%A9%A9%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="拉丁美洲诗歌（页面不存在）">拉丁美洲诗人</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin_American_poetry" title="en:Latin American poetry"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Latin American poetry</span></a></span>）</span></span>包括<a href="/wiki/%E5%A5%A5%E5%85%8B%E5%A1%94%E7%BB%B4%E5%A5%A5%C2%B7%E5%B8%95%E6%96%AF" title="奥克塔维奥·帕斯">奥克塔维奥·帕斯</a>及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Alejandra Pizarnik" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="亚历杭德拉·皮萨尼克"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%9E%E6%AD%B7%E6%9D%AD%E5%BE%B7%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%9A%AE%E8%96%A9%E5%B0%BC%E5%85%8B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="亚历杭德拉·皮萨尼克（页面不存在）">亚历杭德拉·皮萨尼克</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alejandra_Pizarnik" title="en:Alejandra Pizarnik"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Alejandra Pizarnik</span></a></span>）</span></span>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.BC.95.E8.A9.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="轻诗">轻诗</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：轻诗">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Light poetry" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="轻诗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%BC%95%E8%A9%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="轻诗（页面不存在）">轻诗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Light_poetry" title="en:Light poetry"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Light poetry</span></a></span>）</span></span></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1353" data-file-width="957" decoding="async" height="311" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg/220px-LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg/330px-LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg/440px-LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:LewisCarrollSelfPhoto.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E5%8D%A1%E7%BE%85" title="路易斯·卡罗">路易斯·卡罗</a>既是儿童文学作家，亦是轻诗派着名诗人之一</div></div></div>
<p>轻诗是一种用作幽默的诗歌。轻诗之所以称作「轻」是因为这些诗歌通常简短、主题既可为轻浮亦可为严肃，而且经常包含<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%87%E5%AD%97%E6%B8%B8%E6%88%8F" title="文字游戏">文字游戏</a>的元素，如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%99%E9%97%9C%E8%AA%9E" title="双关语">双关语</a>、冒险的押韵及重度的<a href="/wiki/%E9%A0%AD%E9%9F%BB%E6%B3%95" title="头韵法">头韵</a>。虽然少数自由诗人在传统诗体以外的轻诗上不缺出色作品，于英语世界的轻诗至少违反若干正式常规。轻诗的主要形态包括<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Limerick (poetry)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="五行打油诗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%94%E8%A1%8C%E6%89%93%E6%B2%B9%E8%A9%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="五行打油诗（页面不存在）">五行打油诗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limerick_(poetry)" title="en:Limerick (poetry)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Limerick (poetry)</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E8%90%8A%E9%87%8C%E4%BC%91%E8%A9%A9" title="克莱里休诗">克莱里休诗</a>及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Double dactyl" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="双扬抑抑格"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%99%E6%8F%9A%E6%8A%91%E6%8A%91%E6%A0%BC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="双扬抑抑格（页面不存在）">双扬抑抑格</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Double_dactyl" title="en:Double dactyl"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Double dactyl</span></a></span>）</span></span>。
</p><p>虽然轻诗有时候会被贬称为<a href="/wiki/%E6%89%93%E6%B2%B9%E8%A9%A9" title="打油诗">打油诗</a>，又或被称是随意写的诗歌，幽默在轻诗中往往以微妙或颠覆性的方式带出严肃的观点。而不少知名的「严肃派」诗人于轻诗创作上亦有超常发挥。着名轻诗诗人包括<a href="/wiki/%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E5%8D%A1%E7%BE%85" title="路易斯·卡罗">路易斯·卡罗</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ogden Nash" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="奥格登·拿殊"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A5%A7%E6%A0%BC%E7%99%BB%C2%B7%E6%8B%BF%E6%AE%8A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="奥格登·拿殊（页面不存在）">奥格登·拿殊</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ogden_Nash" title="en:Ogden Nash"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ogden Nash</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="X. J. Kennedy" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="X·J·肯尼迪"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=X%C2%B7J%C2%B7%E8%82%AF%E5%B0%BC%E8%BF%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="X·J·肯尼迪（页面不存在）">X·J·肯尼迪</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/X._J._Kennedy" title="en:X. J. Kennedy"><span dir="auto" lang="en">X. J. Kennedy</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Willard R. Espy" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="威拉德·R·艾斯"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A8%81%E6%8B%89%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7R%C2%B7%E8%89%BE%E6%96%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="威拉德·R·艾斯（页面不存在）">威拉德·R·艾斯</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Willard_R._Espy" title="en:Willard R. Espy"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Willard R. Espy</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%B0%A2%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E5%B8%8C%E5%B0%94%E5%BC%97%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6" title="谢尔·希尔弗斯坦">谢尔·希尔弗斯坦</a>及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Wendy Cope" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="温蒂·科普"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%BA%AB%E8%92%82%C2%B7%E7%A7%91%E6%99%AE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="温蒂·科普（页面不存在）">温蒂·科普</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wendy_Cope" title="en:Wendy Cope"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Wendy Cope</span></a></span>）</span></span>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.BB.BF.E8.B2.AB.E8.A9.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="满贯诗">满贯诗</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：满贯诗">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Poetry slam" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="诗歌大满贯"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A9%A9%E6%AD%8C%E5%A4%A7%E6%BB%BF%E8%B2%AB&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="诗歌大满贯（页面不存在）">诗歌大满贯</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poetry_slam" title="en:Poetry slam"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Poetry slam</span></a></span>）</span></span></div>
<p>满贯诗是一种诗歌体裁，源于1986年，<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Marc Smith" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="马克·史密斯"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E5%8F%B2%E5%AF%86%E6%96%AF" title="马克·史密斯">马克·史密斯</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marc_Smith" title="en:Marc Smith"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Marc Smith</span></a></span>）</span></span>于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8A%E5%88%A9%E8%AF%BA%E4%BC%8A%E5%B7%9E" title="伊利诺伊州">伊利诺伊州</a><a href="/wiki/%E8%8A%9D%E5%8A%A0%E5%93%A5" title="芝加哥">芝加哥</a>举办首届诗歌大满贯。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[60]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63"><a href="#cite_note-63">[61]</a></sup>诗歌大满贯中的演绎者在听众面前以情绪化的方式，就个人、社会或其他方面大声评论，而比赛着重文字游戏之美、语调和其抑扬变化。而满贯诗在特定的「<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Poetry slam" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="诗歌大满贯"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A9%A9%E6%AD%8C%E5%A4%A7%E6%BB%BF%E8%B2%AB&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="诗歌大满贯（页面不存在）">诗歌大满贯</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poetry_slam" title="en:Poetry slam"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Poetry slam</span></a></span>）</span></span>」比赛中，通常均具竞争性。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[62]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.8F.BE.E4.BB.A3.E8.A9.A9.E7.88.AD.E8.AB.96"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="现代诗争论">现代诗争论</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：现代诗争论">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>传统诗歌对诗的形式非常看重，形式的运用与发展基本是为了体现诗歌的美感、利于吟诵、和使内容更深刻。但现代诗歌多对格式要求有所放松，一般至少还保留着分行与押韵，或只剩分行。有些分行的“诗歌”，去掉分行后可能仅仅就是篇散文。完全不顾格式的诗歌，实际上已很难认定为诗歌，当然，这牵扯到诗歌的定义及其定义的发展。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.9B.B8.E9.97.9C.E6.A2.9D.E7.9B.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="相关条目">相关条目</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：相关条目">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E5.BB.B6.E4.BC.B8.E9.98.85.E8.AF.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="延伸阅读">延伸阅读</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：延伸阅读">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><span class="mw-editsection-like plainlinks" style="float: right;"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="extiw" href="https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Q482" title="wikidata:Q482"><span class="nomobile">在维基数据</span>编<span class="nomobile">辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span>
</p>

<h2><span id=".E8.A8.BB.E9.87.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注释">注释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：注释">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div id="references-NoteFoot"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">又称「sestet」。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-26"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-26">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">在文学研究中，西方文学中的「行」（line）会被译作「bat」，但在个别形式中，该单位与「wak」会更为相似。为避免引起不必要之误会，本条目将会指「bat」和「wak」而非「line」，当中后者可指前两者。</span>
</li>
</ol></div>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.80.83.E6.96.87.E7.8C.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考文献">参考文献</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="编辑章节：参考文献">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E8.A8.BB.E8.85.B3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注脚">注脚</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AF%97%E6%AD%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：注脚">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-count references-column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2; list-style-type: decimal;">
